OBJECT Report 11020277 Sales Invoice
{
  OBJECT-PROPERTIES
  {
    Date=;
    Time=;
    Version List=4PS14.00;
  }
  PROPERTIES
  {
    Permissions=TableData 7190=rimd;
    CaptionML=[DEU=Verkauf - Rechnung;
               ENU=Sales - Invoice;
               NLD=Verkoop - Factuur;
               NOR=Salg - faktura;
               SVE=F”rs.faktura];
    OnInitReport=BEGIN
                   GLSetup.GET;
                   SalesSetup.GET;
                   CompanyInfo.GET;
                   CompanyInfo.CALCFIELDS(Picture);
                   JobsSetup.GET;
                 END;

    OnPreReport=BEGIN
                  IF NOT CurrReport.USEREQUESTPAGE THEN
                    InitLogInteraction;
                END;

  }
  DATASET
  {
    { 1100525000;;DataItem;                  ;
               DataItemTable=Table112;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(No.);
               ReqFilterHeadingML=[DEU=Geb. Verkaufsrechnung;
                                   ENU=Posted Sales Invoice;
                                   NLD=Geboekte verkoopfactuur;
                                   NOR=Bokf›rt salgsfaktura;
                                   SVE=Bokf”rd f”rs„ljningsfaktura];
               OnPreDataItem=BEGIN
                               DPA_SetFilters(CurrReport.OBJECTID(FALSE));
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  CurrReport.LANGUAGE := Language.GetLanguageID("Language Code");

                                  IF RespCenter.GET("Responsibility Center") THEN BEGIN
                                    FormatAddr.RespCenter(CompanyAddr,RespCenter);
                                    CompanyInfo."Phone No." := RespCenter."Phone No.";
                                    CompanyInfo."Fax No." := RespCenter."Fax No.";
                                  END ELSE
                                    FormatAddr.Company(CompanyAddr,CompanyInfo);

                                  CheckDimensionAddress("Shortcut Dimension 1 Code");

                                  IF "Order No." = '' THEN
                                    OrderNoText := ''
                                  ELSE
                                    OrderNoText := FIELDCAPTION("Order No.");
                                  IF "Salesperson Code" = '' THEN BEGIN
                                    SalesPurchPerson.INIT;
                                    SalesPersonText := '';
                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                    SalesPurchPerson.GET("Salesperson Code");
                                    SalesPersonText := Text000;
                                  END;
                                  IF "Your Reference" = '' THEN
                                    ReferenceText := ''
                                  ELSE
                                    ReferenceText := FIELDCAPTION("Your Reference");
                                  IF "Principal Reference" = '' THEN
                                    PrincipalReferenceText := ''
                                  ELSE
                                    PrincipalReferenceText := FIELDCAPTION("Principal Reference");
                                  IF "VAT Registration No." = '' THEN
                                    VATNoText := ''
                                  ELSE
                                    VATNoText := FIELDCAPTION("VAT Registration No.");
                                  IF "Currency Code" = '' THEN BEGIN
                                    GLSetup.TESTFIELD("LCY Code");
                                    TotalText := STRSUBSTNO(Text001,GLSetup."LCY Code");
                                    TotalInclVATText := STRSUBSTNO(Text002,GLSetup."LCY Code");
                                    TotalExclVATText := STRSUBSTNO(Text006,GLSetup."LCY Code");
                                    CurrencyCode := GLSetup."LCY Code";
                                    AmountRoundingPrecision := GLSetup."Amount Rounding Precision";
                                  END ELSE BEGIN
                                    TotalText := STRSUBSTNO(Text001,"Currency Code");
                                    TotalInclVATText := STRSUBSTNO(Text002,"Currency Code");
                                    TotalExclVATText := STRSUBSTNO(Text006,"Currency Code");
                                    CurrencyCode := "Currency Code";
                                    Currency.GET("Currency Code");
                                    AmountRoundingPrecision := Currency."Amount Rounding Precision";
                                  END;
                                  FormatAddr.SalesInvBillTo(CustAddr,"Sales Invoice Header");
                                  IF NOT Cust.GET("Bill-to Customer No.") THEN
                                    CLEAR(Cust);

                                  IF "Payment Terms Code" = '' THEN
                                    PaymentTerms.INIT
                                  ELSE BEGIN
                                    PaymentTerms.GET("Payment Terms Code");
                                    PaymentTerms.TranslateDescription(PaymentTerms,"Language Code");
                                  END;
                                  IF "Shipment Method Code" = '' THEN
                                    ShipmentMethod.INIT
                                  ELSE BEGIN
                                    ShipmentMethod.GET("Shipment Method Code");
                                    ShipmentMethod.TranslateDescription(ShipmentMethod,"Language Code");
                                  END;

                                  ShowShippingAddr := FormatAddr.SalesInvShipTo(ShipToAddr,CustAddr,"Sales Invoice Header");

                                  ShowShippingAddr := FALSE; // not used

                                  IF LogInteraction THEN
                                    IF NOT CurrReport.PREVIEW THEN BEGIN
                                      IF "Bill-to Contact No." <> '' THEN
                                        SegManagement.LogDocument(
                                          4,"No.",0,0,DATABASE::Contact,"Bill-to Contact No.","Salesperson Code",
                                          "Campaign No.","Posting Description",'')
                                      ELSE
                                        SegManagement.LogDocument(
                                          4,"No.",0,0,DATABASE::Customer,"Bill-to Customer No.","Salesperson Code",
                                          "Campaign No.","Posting Description",'');
                                    END;

                                  FillJobInfo;

                                  CALCFIELDS("Amount Including VAT");
                                  "Credit Restriction Amount" := "Amount Including VAT" * ("Credit Restriction %" / 100);
                                  CreditRestrictionText := STRSUBSTNO(Text11020254, FORMAT("Credit Restriction %") + '%');

                                  IF "WKA Period" = '' THEN
                                    WKAPeriodText := ''
                                  ELSE
                                    WKAPeriodText := FIELDCAPTION("WKA Period");

                                  CommentOnPayment := STRSUBSTNO(Text11012004, "Bill-to Customer No.", "No.");

                                  IF CompanyInfo."Phone No. Accounts Department" = '' THEN
                                    PhoneNoAccountsDepartment := ''
                                  ELSE
                                    PhoneNoAccountsDepartment := STRSUBSTNO(Text11012005, CompanyInfo."Phone No. Accounts Department");

                                  Invoiced := 0;
                                  ContractAmount := 0;
                                  ToBeInvoiced := 0;
                                  IF PrintPaymentProgress THEN
                                    CalcSummary("Sales Invoice Header");

                                  PrintLogo :=
                                    (SalesSetup."Logo Position on Documents" <> SalesSetup."Logo Position on Documents"::"No Logo") AND
                                    ("E-Mail (Invoices)" <> '') AND
                                    ("Electronic Invoicing" = "Sales Invoice Header"."Electronic Invoicing"::"E-Mail");
                                END;

               ReqFilterFields=No.,Sell-to Customer No.,No. Printed,Inserted By }

    { 1100525001;1;DataItem;CopyLoop         ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number);
               OnPreDataItem=VAR
                               NoOfLoops@1100525000 : Integer;
                             BEGIN
                               NoOfLoops := ABS(NoOfCopies) + Cust."Invoice Copies" + 1;
                               NoOfLoops := NoOfLoops + GetPlantLocationInvoiceCopies;
                               IF NoOfLoops <= 0 THEN
                                 NoOfLoops := 1;
                               CopyText := '';
                               SETRANGE(Number, 1, NoOfLoops);
                               OutputNo := 1;
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  IF Number > 1 THEN BEGIN
                                    CopyText := Text003;
                                    OutputNo += 1;
                                  END;

                                  LastServiceOrderNo := '';
                                  LastServiceContractNo := '';
                                  ServiceOrder."No." := '';
                                  ServiceContract."No." := '';

                                  LastRentalUnit := '';
                                  LastRentalPeriod := '';
                                  RentalUnit."Rental Unit" := ''
                                END;

               OnPostDataItem=BEGIN
                                IF NOT CurrReport.PREVIEW THEN
                                  SalesInvCountPrinted.RUN("Sales Invoice Header");
                              END;
                               }

    { 1100525002;2;DataItem;PageLoop         ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number)
                                 WHERE(Number=CONST(1)) }

    { 1100525025;3;Column;OutputNo_PageLoop  ;
               SourceExpr=OutputNo }

    { 1100525005;3;DataItem;                 ;
               DataItemTable=Table113;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Document No.,Line No.);
               OnPreDataItem=VAR
                               MoreLines@1100525000 : Boolean;
                             BEGIN
                               VATAmountLine.DELETEALL;
                               SalesShipmentBuffer.RESET;
                               SalesShipmentBuffer.DELETEALL;
                               FirstValueEntryNo := 0;
                               MoreLines := FIND('+');
                               WHILE MoreLines AND (Description = '') AND ("No." = '') AND (Quantity = 0) AND (Amount = 0) DO
                                 MoreLines := NEXT(-1) <> 0;
                               IF NOT MoreLines THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;
                               SETRANGE("Line No.", 0, "Line No.");
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  PostedShipmentDate := 0D;
                                  IF Quantity <> 0 THEN
                                    PostedShipmentDate := FindPostedShipmentDate;

                                  IF (Type = Type::"G/L Account") AND (NOT ShowInternalInfo) THEN
                                    "No." := '';

                                  VATAmountLine.INIT;
                                  VATAmountLine."VAT Identifier" := "VAT Identifier";
                                  VATAmountLine."VAT Calculation Type" := "VAT Calculation Type";
                                  VATAmountLine."Tax Group Code" := "Tax Group Code";
                                  VATAmountLine."VAT %" := "VAT %";
                                  VATAmountLine."VAT Base" := Amount;
                                  VATAmountLine."Amount Including VAT" := "Amount Including VAT";
                                  VATAmountLine."Line Amount" := "Line Amount";
                                  IF "Allow Invoice Disc." THEN
                                    VATAmountLine."Inv. Disc. Base Amount" := "Line Amount";
                                  VATAmountLine."Invoice Discount Amount" := "Inv. Discount Amount";
                                  VATAmountLine."Reverse Charge VAT" := ("VAT Calculation Type" = "VAT Calculation Type"::"Reverse Charge VAT");
                                  VATAmountLine.InsertLine;

                                  IF Type = Type::" " THEN BEGIN
                                    IF "Service Order No." <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                      IF "Service Order No." = LastServiceOrderNo THEN
                                        ServiceOrder."No." := ''
                                      ELSE BEGIN
                                        ServiceOrder.GET("Service Order No.");
                                        LastServiceOrderNo := ServiceOrder."No.";
                                      END;
                                    END ELSE BEGIN
                                      IF "Service Contract No." <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                        IF "Service Contract No." = LastServiceContractNo THEN
                                          ServiceContract."No." := ''
                                        ELSE BEGIN
                                          ServiceContract.GET("Service Contract No.");
                                          LastServiceContractNo := ServiceContract."No.";
                                        END;
                                      END;
                                    END;
                                  END;

                                  IF "Rental Unit Invoice" AND JobsSetup."Rental Units active" THEN BEGIN
                                    IF "Rental Unit" <> '' THEN BEGIN
                                      IF ("Rental Unit" = LastRentalUnit) AND ("Rental Period" = LastRentalPeriod) THEN
                                        RentalUnit."Rental Unit" := ''
                                      ELSE BEGIN
                                        IF NOT RentalUnit.GET("Job No.", "Rental Unit") THEN
                                          CLEAR(RentalUnit);
                                        LastRentalUnit := "Rental Unit";
                                        LastRentalPeriod := "Rental Period";
                                      END;
                                    END;
                                  END;
                                END;

               DataItemLinkReference=Sales Invoice Header;
               DataItemLink=Document No.=FIELD(No.) }

    { 1100525035;3;DataItem;VATCounterLCY    ;
               DataItemTable=Table2000000026;
               DataItemTableView=SORTING(Number);
               OnPreDataItem=VAR
                               CalculatedExchRate@1100525000 : Decimal;
                             BEGIN
                               IF (NOT GLSetup."Print VAT specification in LCY") OR
                                  ("Sales Invoice Header"."Currency Code" = '') OR
                                  (VATAmountLine.COUNT <= 1)
                               THEN
                                 CurrReport.BREAK;

                               SETRANGE(Number, 1, VATAmountLine.COUNT);

                               IF GLSetup."LCY Code" = '' THEN
                                 VALSpecLCYHeader := Text007 + Text008
                               ELSE
                                 VALSpecLCYHeader := Text007 + FORMAT(GLSetup."LCY Code");

                               CurrExchRate.FindCurrency(0, '', "Sales Invoice Header"."Posting Date", "Sales Invoice Header"."Currency Code", 1);
                               CalculatedExchRate := ROUND(1 / "Sales Invoice Header"."Currency Factor" * CurrExchRate."Exchange Rate Amount", 0.000001);
                               VALExchRate := STRSUBSTNO(Text009, CalculatedExchRate, CurrExchRate."Exchange Rate Amount");
                             END;

               OnAfterGetRecord=BEGIN
                                  VATAmountLine.GetLine(Number);

                                  VALVATBaseLCY := ROUND(VATAmountLine."VAT Base" / "Sales Invoice Header"."Currency Factor");
                                  VALVATAmountLCY := ROUND(VATAmountLine."VAT Amount" / "Sales Invoice Header"."Currency Factor");
                                END;
                                 }

    { 1100525131;4;Column;Number_VATCounterLCY;
               SourceExpr=VATCounterLCY.Number }

               SourceExpr=VALSpecLCYHeader }

      TextContinued@1100525124 : TextConst 'DEU=Fortsetzung;ENU=Continued;NLD=Transport;NOR=Fortsettes;SVE=Forts„ttning';

    PROCEDURE InitLogInteraction@1();
    BEGIN
      LogInteraction := SegManagement.FindInteractTmplCode(4) <> '';
    END;

    PROCEDURE FindPostedShipmentDate@6() : Date;
    VAR
      SalesShipmentHeader@1000 : Record 110;
      SalesShipmentBuffer2@1001 : TEMPORARY Record 7190;
    BEGIN
      NextEntryNo := 1;
      IF "Sales Invoice Line"."Shipment No." <> '' THEN
        IF SalesShipmentHeader.GET("Sales Invoice Line"."Shipment No.") THEN
          EXIT(SalesShipmentHeader."Posting Date");

      IF "Sales Invoice Header"."Order No."='' THEN
        EXIT("Sales Invoice Header"."Posting Date");

      CASE "Sales Invoice Line".Type OF
        "Sales Invoice Line".Type::Item:
          GenerateBufferFromValueEntry("Sales Invoice Line");
        "Sales Invoice Line".Type::"G/L Account","Sales Invoice Line".Type::Resource,
        "Sales Invoice Line".Type::"Charge (Item)","Sales Invoice Line".Type::"Fixed Asset":
           GenerateBufferFromShipment("Sales Invoice Line");
        "Sales Invoice Line".Type::" ":
            EXIT(0D);
      END;

      SalesShipmentBuffer.RESET;
      SalesShipmentBuffer.SETRANGE("Document No.","Sales Invoice Line"."Document No.");
      SalesShipmentBuffer.SETRANGE("Line No.","Sales Invoice Line"."Line No.");
      IF SalesShipmentBuffer.FIND('-') THEN BEGIN
        SalesShipmentBuffer2 := SalesShipmentBuffer;
        IF SalesShipmentBuffer.NEXT = 0 THEN BEGIN
          SalesShipmentBuffer.GET(
            SalesShipmentBuffer2."Document No.",SalesShipmentBuffer2."Line No.",SalesShipmentBuffer2."Entry No.");
          SalesShipmentBuffer.DELETE;
          EXIT(SalesShipmentBuffer2."Posting Date");
        END ;
        SalesShipmentBuffer.CALCSUMS(Quantity);
        IF SalesShipmentBuffer.Quantity <> "Sales Invoice Line".Quantity THEN BEGIN
          SalesShipmentBuffer.DELETEALL;
          EXIT("Sales Invoice Header"."Posting Date");
        END;
      END ELSE
        EXIT("Sales Invoice Header"."Posting Date");
    END;

    PROCEDURE GenerateBufferFromValueEntry@2(SalesInvoiceLine2@1002 : Record 113);
    VAR
      ValueEntry@1000 : Record 5802;
      ItemLedgerEntry@1001 : Record 32;
      TotalQuantity@1003 : Decimal;
      Quantity@1004 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      TotalQuantity := SalesInvoiceLine2."Quantity (Base)";
      ValueEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Document No.");
      ValueEntry.SETRANGE("Document No.",SalesInvoiceLine2."Document No.");
      ValueEntry.SETRANGE("Posting Date","Sales Invoice Header"."Posting Date");
      ValueEntry.SETRANGE("Item Charge No.",'');
      ValueEntry.SETFILTER("Entry No.",'%1..',FirstValueEntryNo);
      IF ValueEntry.FIND('-') THEN
        REPEAT
          IF ItemLedgerEntry.GET(ValueEntry."Item Ledger Entry No.") THEN BEGIN
            IF SalesInvoiceLine2."Qty. per Unit of Measure" <> 0 THEN
              Quantity := ValueEntry."Invoiced Quantity" / SalesInvoiceLine2."Qty. per Unit of Measure"
            ELSE
              Quantity := ValueEntry."Invoiced Quantity";
            AddBufferEntry(
              SalesInvoiceLine2,
              -Quantity,
              ItemLedgerEntry."Posting Date");
            TotalQuantity := TotalQuantity + ValueEntry."Invoiced Quantity";
          END;
          FirstValueEntryNo := ValueEntry."Entry No." + 1;
        UNTIL (ValueEntry.NEXT = 0) OR (TotalQuantity = 0);
    END;

    PROCEDURE GenerateBufferFromShipment@8(SalesInvoiceLine@1000 : Record 113);
    VAR
      SalesInvoiceHeader@1001 : Record 112;
      SalesInvoiceLine2@1002 : Record 113;
      SalesShipmentHeader@1006 : Record 110;
      SalesShipmentLine@1004 : Record 111;
      TotalQuantity@1003 : Decimal;
      Quantity@1005 : Decimal;
    BEGIN
      TotalQuantity := 0;
      SalesInvoiceHeader.SETCURRENTKEY("Order No.");
      SalesInvoiceHeader.SETFILTER("No.",'..%1',"Sales Invoice Header"."No.");
      SalesInvoiceHeader.SETRANGE("Order No.","Sales Invoice Header"."Order No.");
      IF SalesInvoiceHeader.FIND('-') THEN
        REPEAT
          SalesInvoiceLine2.SETRANGE("Document No.",SalesInvoiceHeader."No.");
          SalesInvoiceLine2.SETRANGE("Line No.",SalesInvoiceLine."Line No.");
          SalesInvoiceLine2.SETRANGE(Type,SalesInvoiceLine.Type);
          SalesInvoiceLine2.SETRANGE("No.",SalesInvoiceLine."No.");
          SalesInvoiceLine2.SETRANGE("Unit of Measure Code",SalesInvoiceLine."Unit of Measure Code");
          IF SalesInvoiceLine2.FIND('-') THEN
            REPEAT
              TotalQuantity := TotalQuantity + SalesInvoiceLine2.Quantity;
            UNTIL SalesInvoiceLine2.NEXT = 0;
        UNTIL SalesInvoiceHeader.NEXT = 0;

      SalesShipmentLine.SETCURRENTKEY("Order No.","Order Line No.");
      SalesShipmentLine.SETRANGE("Order No.","Sales Invoice Header"."Order No.");
      SalesShipmentLine.SETRANGE("Order Line No.",SalesInvoiceLine."Line No.");
      SalesShipmentLine.SETRANGE("Line No.",SalesInvoiceLine."Line No.");
      SalesShipmentLine.SETRANGE(Type,SalesInvoiceLine.Type);
      SalesShipmentLine.SETRANGE("No.",SalesInvoiceLine."No.");
      SalesShipmentLine.SETRANGE("Unit of Measure Code",SalesInvoiceLine."Unit of Measure Code");
      SalesShipmentLine.SETFILTER(Quantity,'<>%1',0);

      IF SalesShipmentLine.FIND('-') THEN
        REPEAT
          IF "Sales Invoice Header"."Get Shipment Used" THEN
            CorrectShipment(SalesShipmentLine);
          IF ABS(SalesShipmentLine.Quantity) <= ABS(TotalQuantity - SalesInvoiceLine.Quantity) THEN
            TotalQuantity := TotalQuantity - SalesShipmentLine.Quantity
          ELSE BEGIN
            IF ABS(SalesShipmentLine.Quantity)  > ABS(TotalQuantity) THEN
              SalesShipmentLine.Quantity := TotalQuantity;
            Quantity :=
              SalesShipmentLine.Quantity - (TotalQuantity - SalesInvoiceLine.Quantity);

            TotalQuantity := TotalQuantity - SalesShipmentLine.Quantity;
            SalesInvoiceLine.Quantity := SalesInvoiceLine.Quantity - Quantity;

            IF SalesShipmentHeader.GET(SalesShipmentLine."Document No.") THEN
              AddBufferEntry(
                SalesInvoiceLine,
                Quantity,
                SalesShipmentHeader."Posting Date");
          END;
        UNTIL (SalesShipmentLine.NEXT = 0) OR (TotalQuantity = 0);
    END;

    PROCEDURE CorrectShipment@7(VAR SalesShipmentLine@1001 : Record 111);
    VAR
      SalesInvoiceLine@1000 : Record 113;
    BEGIN
      SalesInvoiceLine.SETCURRENTKEY("Shipment No.","Shipment Line No.");
      SalesInvoiceLine.SETRANGE("Shipment No.",SalesShipmentLine."Document No.");
      SalesInvoiceLine.SETRANGE("Shipment Line No.",SalesShipmentLine."Line No.");
      IF SalesInvoiceLine.FIND('-') THEN
        REPEAT
          SalesShipmentLine.Quantity := SalesShipmentLine.Quantity - SalesInvoiceLine.Quantity;
        UNTIL SalesInvoiceLine.NEXT = 0;
    END;

    PROCEDURE AddBufferEntry@3(SalesInvoiceLine@1001 : Record 113;QtyOnShipment@1002 : Decimal;PostingDate@1003 : Date);
    BEGIN
      SalesShipmentBuffer.SETRANGE("Document No.",SalesInvoiceLine."Document No.");
      SalesShipmentBuffer.SETRANGE("Line No.",SalesInvoiceLine."Line No.");
      SalesShipmentBuffer.SETRANGE("Posting Date",PostingDate);
      IF SalesShipmentBuffer.FIND('-') THEN BEGIN
        SalesShipmentBuffer.Quantity := SalesShipmentBuffer.Quantity + QtyOnShipment;
        SalesShipmentBuffer.MODIFY;
        EXIT;
      END;

      WITH SalesShipmentBuffer DO BEGIN
        "Document No." := SalesInvoiceLine."Document No.";
        "Line No." := SalesInvoiceLine."Line No.";
        "Entry No." := NextEntryNo;
        Type := SalesInvoiceLine.Type;
        "No." := SalesInvoiceLine."No.";
        Quantity := QtyOnShipment;
       "Posting Date" := PostingDate;
        INSERT;
        NextEntryNo := NextEntryNo + 1
      END;
    END;

    LOCAL PROCEDURE DocumentCaption@4() : Text[250];
    BEGIN
      IF "Sales Invoice Header"."Prepayment Invoice" THEN
        EXIT(Text010);
      EXIT(Text004);
    END;

    PROCEDURE InitializeRequest@5(NewNoOfCopies@1000 : Integer;NewShowInternalInfo@1001 : Boolean;NewLogInteraction@1002 : Boolean;DisplayAsmInfo@1003 : Boolean);
    BEGIN
      NoOfCopies := NewNoOfCopies;
      ShowInternalInfo := NewShowInternalInfo;
      LogInteraction := NewLogInteraction;
      //DisplayAssemblyInformation := DisplayAsmInfo; // mboers
    END;

    PROCEDURE FillJobInfo@11012000();
    VAR
      SalesInvoiceLine@11012001 : Record 113;
      Customer@1100525001 : Record 18;
      CustomerBankAccount@1100525000 : Record 287;
      AutoFormatManagement@11012003 : Codeunit 45;
      AmountFormat@11012002 : Text[50];
    BEGIN
      ProjectText := '';
      ProjectNoText := '';
      ProjectDescText := '';

      CLEAR(Job);
      IF "Sales Invoice Header"."Plant Invoice" AND ("Sales Invoice Header"."Company Name" <> '') THEN
        Job.CHANGECOMPANY("Sales Invoice Header"."Company Name")
      ELSE
        Job.CHANGECOMPANY(COMPANYNAME);

      IF "Sales Invoice Header"."Job No." <> '' THEN
        Job.GET("Sales Invoice Header"."Job No.")
      ELSE BEGIN
        SalesInvoiceLine.SETRANGE("Document No.", "Sales Invoice Header"."No.");
        SalesInvoiceLine.SETFILTER("Job No.", '<>%1', '');
        SalesInvoiceLine.SETFILTER(Type, '<>%1', SalesInvoiceLine.Type::" ");
        IF SalesInvoiceLine.FINDSET THEN
          Job.GET(SalesInvoiceLine."Job No.");
      END;

      IF Job.RAW THEN
        PrintPaymentProgress := FALSE; //bij RAW vindt er achteraf een verrekening plaats

      ProjectText := "Sales Invoice Header".FIELDCAPTION("Job No.");
      ProjectNoText := Job."No.";
      ProjectDescText := Job.Description;

      RentalPeriodText := '';
      IF "Sales Invoice Header"."Plant Invoice" AND ("Sales Invoice Header"."Rental Period to Date" <> 0D) THEN
        RentalPeriodText := "Sales Invoice Header".FIELDCAPTION("Rental Period to Date");

      "Sales Invoice Header".CALCFIELDS("Amount Including VAT");

      AmountFormat := AutoFormatManagement.AutoFormatTranslate(1, CurrencyCode);

      Remit1Text := '';
      Remit2Text := '';
      Remit3Text := '';
      Remit4Text := '';
      Remit5Text := '';

      LaborAmountText := FORMAT("Sales Invoice Header"."Labor Amount (Subcontracting)", 0, AmountFormat);
      LaborPartText := STRSUBSTNO(Text11012000, "Sales Invoice Header"."% Labor", LaborAmountText);
      BlockedAmountText := FORMAT("Sales Invoice Header"."Blocked Amount (Subcontracting", 0, AmountFormat);
      RestAmountText := FORMAT("Sales Invoice Header"."Amount Including VAT" - "Sales Invoice Header"."Blocked Amount (Subcontracting", 0, AmountFormat);
      BAccountText := STRSUBSTNO(Text11012001, "Sales Invoice Header"."% to B Account", BlockedAmountText);
      Remit2Text := STRSUBSTNO(Text11012002, CurrencyCode, BlockedAmountText, CompanyInfo."B-Account");

      WithholdAmountText := '';
      IF "Sales Invoice Header"."Withhold % Last Installment" = 0 THEN BEGIN
        RestAmountText := FORMAT("Sales Invoice Header"."Amount Including VAT" - "Sales Invoice Header"."Blocked Amount (Subcontracting", 0, AmountFormat);
      END ELSE BEGIN
        "Sales Invoice Header".CALCFIELDS("Last Installment Amount");
        RestAmountText := FORMAT(
          "Sales Invoice Header"."Amount Including VAT" - "Sales Invoice Header"."Blocked Amount (Subcontracting" -
          (("Sales Invoice Header"."Last Installment Amount" / 100) * "Sales Invoice Header"."Withhold % Last Installment"),
          0, AmountFormat);
        LastInstallmentAmountText := FORMAT("Sales Invoice Header"."Last Installment Amount", 0, AmountFormat);
        WithholdAmountText := FORMAT(
          ("Sales Invoice Header"."Last Installment Amount" / 100) * "Sales Invoice Header"."Withhold % Last Installment",
          0, AmountFormat);
        Customer.GET("Sales Invoice Header"."Public notary");
        CustomerBankAccount.GET(Customer."No.", Customer."Preferred Bank Account Code");
        Remit3Text := STRSUBSTNO(
          Text11012007, CurrencyCode, WithholdAmountText, CustomerBankAccount."Bank Account No.",
          Customer.Name, Customer.City);
        Remit4Text := STRSUBSTNO(Text11012009, "Sales Invoice Header"."Notary Case Number");
        Remit5Text := STRSUBSTNO(Text11012008, "Sales Invoice Header"."Withhold % Last Installment", CurrencyCode, LastInstallmentAmountText);
      END;

      Remit1Text := STRSUBSTNO(
        Text11012003, CurrencyCode, RestAmountText, CompanyInfo."Bank Account No.", CompanyInfo."Giro No.");
    END;

    PROCEDURE CheckDimensionAddress@1100485005(Dim1Code@1100485003 : Code[20]);
    VAR
      Contact@1100485002 : Record 5050;
      DimensionValue@1100485001 : Record 349;
      DimensionManagement@1100485000 : Codeunit 408;
    BEGIN
      IF Dim1Code <> '' THEN BEGIN
        DimensionManagement.GetDimValueRec(1, Dim1Code, DimensionValue, TRUE, '');
        IF DimensionValue."Contact No. (Company)" <> '' THEN BEGIN
          Contact.GET(DimensionValue."Contact No. (Company)");
          FormatAddr.ContactAddr(CompanyAddr, Contact);
        END;
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE CalcSummary@1100485002(SalesInvoiceHeader@1100485000 : Record 112);
    VAR
      SalesInvoiceLine@1100525001 : Record 113;
      ProjectInstallment@1100525002 : Record 11012018;
      TempPlot@1100525000 : TEMPORARY Record 11012500;
    BEGIN
      //Bepalen aanneemsom en gefactureerd
      //Uitgangspunten:
      // - op een factuur alleen termijnen van zelfde type (Project/Bouwnummer/MMW)
      // - voor MMW contracten in principe geen summary afdrukken (kan hieronder uit commentaar worden gehaald)
      // - voor optie termijnen nooit een summary afdrukken
      IF SalesInvoiceHeader."Installment Invoice" AND NOT SalesInvoiceHeader."Service Invoice" THEN BEGIN
        Invoiced := 0;
        ContractAmount := 0;
        PresentEntryNo := 0;
        PresentEntryNo := DetermineCustomerLedgerNo(CustLedgerEntry."Document Type"::Invoice, SalesInvoiceHeader."No.", SalesInvoiceHeader."Bill-to Customer No.");

        SalesInvoiceLine.RESET;
        SalesInvoiceLine.SETRANGE("Document No.", SalesInvoiceHeader."No.");
        SalesInvoiceLine.SETFILTER(Type, '<>%1', SalesInvoiceLine.Type::" ");
        SalesInvoiceLine.SETRANGE(Option, '');
        SalesInvoiceLine.SETRANGE("Extension Contract", '');
        IF SalesInvoiceLine.FINDSET THEN BEGIN
          IF ProjectInstallment.GET(
            SalesInvoiceHeader."Job No.",
            SalesInvoiceHeader."Sell-to Customer No.",
            SalesInvoiceLine."Plot No.",
            SalesInvoiceLine."Installment No.")
          THEN BEGIN
            CASE TRUE OF
              ((ProjectInstallment."Plot No." <> '') AND (ProjectInstallment.Option = '') AND (ProjectInstallment."Extension Contract" = '')):
                BEGIN
                  SalesInvoiceLine.SETFILTER("Plot No.", '<>%1', '');
                  REPEAT
                    IF NOT TempPlot.GET(SalesInvoiceHeader."Job No.", SalesInvoiceLine."Plot No.") THEN BEGIN
                      IF ProjectInstallment.GET(
                        SalesInvoiceHeader."Job No.",
                        SalesInvoiceHeader."Sell-to Customer No.",
                        SalesInvoiceLine."Plot No.",
                        SalesInvoiceLine."Installment No.")
                      THEN BEGIN
                        IF (ProjectInstallment.Option = '') AND (ProjectInstallment."Extension Contract" = '') THEN BEGIN
                          DeterminePlotSummary(ProjectInstallment."Plot No.");
                          TempPlot."Project No." := SalesInvoiceHeader."Job No.";
                          TempPlot."Plot No." := SalesInvoiceLine."Plot No.";
                          TempPlot.INSERT;
                        END;
                      END;
                    END;
                  UNTIL SalesInvoiceLine.NEXT = 0;
                END;
              ((ProjectInstallment."Plot No." = '') AND (ProjectInstallment.Option = '') AND (ProjectInstallment."Extension Contract" = '')):
                DetermineBasicSummary;
            END;
          END;
        END;

        SalesInvoiceHeader.CALCFIELDS(Amount, "Amount Including VAT");
        ToBeInvoiced := ContractAmount - (Invoiced + SalesInvoiceHeader.Amount);
      END;
    END;

    PROCEDURE DetermineBasicSummary@1100525004();
    VAR
      ProjectPrincipal@1210190000 : Record 11012005;
      ProjectInstallment@1100525000 : Record 11012018;
    BEGIN
      ProjectPrincipal.GET(Job."No.", "Sales Invoice Header"."Sell-to Customer No.");
      ContractAmount := ProjectPrincipal."Contract Amount (LCY)" + ProjectPrincipal."Plot Price";

      ProjectInstallment.SETRANGE("Project No.", Job."No.");
      ProjectInstallment.SETRANGE(Principal, "Sales Invoice Header"."Sell-to Customer No.");
      ProjectInstallment.SETFILTER("Extension Contract", '%1', '');
      ProjectInstallment.SETFILTER(Option, '%1', '');
      ProjectInstallment.SETFILTER("Plot No.", '%1', '');
      IF ProjectInstallment.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          ProjectInstallment.CALCFIELDS("Invoiced Price (LCY)");
          DetermineInvoiced(ProjectInstallment);
        UNTIL ProjectInstallment.NEXT = 0;
    END;

    PROCEDURE DetermineExtensionSummary@1100525002(ExtensionContract@1100485000 : Code[10]);
    VAR
      ProjectInstallment@1100525000 : Record 11012018;
    BEGIN
      ProjectInstallment.SETRANGE("Project No.", Job."No.");
      ProjectInstallment.SETRANGE(Principal, "Sales Invoice Header"."Sell-to Customer No.");
      ProjectInstallment.SETFILTER("Extension Contract", ExtensionContract);
      IF ProjectInstallment.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          ProjectInstallment.CALCFIELDS("Invoiced Price (LCY)");
          ContractAmount := ContractAmount + ProjectInstallment."Installment Amount (LCY)";
          DetermineInvoiced(ProjectInstallment);
        UNTIL ProjectInstallment.NEXT = 0;
    END;

    PROCEDURE DeterminePlotSummary@1100485004(PlotNo@1100485000 : Code[10]);
    VAR
      ProjectInstallment@1100525000 : Record 11012018;
    BEGIN
      ProjectInstallment.SETRANGE("Project No.", Job."No.");
      ProjectInstallment.SETRANGE(Principal, "Sales Invoice Header"."Sell-to Customer No.");
      ProjectInstallment.SETFILTER("Plot No.", PlotNo);
      ProjectInstallment.SETFILTER(Option, '%1', '');
      IF ProjectInstallment.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          ProjectInstallment.CALCFIELDS("Invoiced Price (LCY)");
          ContractAmount := ContractAmount + ProjectInstallment."Installment Amount (LCY)";
          DetermineInvoiced(ProjectInstallment);
        UNTIL ProjectInstallment.NEXT = 0;
    END;

    PROCEDURE DetermineInvoiced@1210190008(ProjectInstallment@1100525000 : Record 11012018);
    VAR
      SalesInvoiceLine@1210190002 : Record 113;
      SalesCrMemoLine@1210190001 : Record 115;
    BEGIN
      SalesInvoiceLine.SETCURRENTKEY("Job No.","Project Invoice","Installment Invoice","Sell-to Customer No.");
      SalesInvoiceLine.SETRANGE("Job No.", Job."No.");
      SalesInvoiceLine.SETRANGE("Sell-to Customer No.", "Sales Invoice Header"."Sell-to Customer No.");
      SalesInvoiceLine.SETRANGE("Project Invoice", TRUE);
      SalesInvoiceLine.SETRANGE("Installment Invoice", TRUE);
      SalesInvoiceLine.SETRANGE("Installment No.", ProjectInstallment."Installment No.");
      SalesInvoiceLine.SETRANGE("Extension Contract", ProjectInstallment."Extension Contract");
      SalesInvoiceLine.SETRANGE("Plot No.", ProjectInstallment."Plot No.");
      IF SalesInvoiceLine.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          InvoiceEntryNo := DetermineCustomerLedgerNo(CustLedgerEntry."Document Type"::Invoice, SalesInvoiceLine."Document No.", "Sales Invoice Header"."Bill-to Customer No.");
          IF InvoiceEntryNo < PresentEntryNo THEN
            Invoiced := Invoiced + SalesInvoiceLine."Amount (LCY)";
        UNTIL SalesInvoiceLine.NEXT = 0;

      SalesCrMemoLine.SETRANGE("Job No.", Job."No.");
      SalesCrMemoLine.SETRANGE("Project Credit Memo", TRUE);
      SalesCrMemoLine.SETRANGE("Sell-to Customer No.", "Sales Invoice Header"."Sell-to Customer No.");
      SalesCrMemoLine.SETRANGE("Installment Credit Memo", TRUE);
      SalesCrMemoLine.SETRANGE("Installment No.", ProjectInstallment."Installment No.");
      SalesCrMemoLine.SETRANGE("Extension Contract", ProjectInstallment."Extension Contract");
      SalesCrMemoLine.SETRANGE("Plot No.", ProjectInstallment."Plot No.");
      IF SalesCrMemoLine.FINDSET THEN
        REPEAT
          InvoiceEntryNo := DetermineCustomerLedgerNo(CustLedgerEntry."Document Type"::"Credit Memo", SalesCrMemoLine."Document No.", "Sales Invoice Header"."Bill-to Customer No.");
          IF InvoiceEntryNo < PresentEntryNo THEN
            Invoiced := Invoiced - SalesCrMemoLine."Amount (LCY)";
        UNTIL SalesCrMemoLine.NEXT = 0;
    END;

    PROCEDURE DetermineCustomerLedgerNo@1210190004(DocumentType@1210190002 : Option;DocumentNo@1210190001 : Code[20];BilltoCustomerNo@1100525000 : Code[20]) @1210190003 : Integer;
    VAR
      CustLedgerEntry@1210190000 : Record 21;
    BEGIN
      CustLedgerEntry.SETCURRENTKEY("Document No.");
      CustLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Document Type", DocumentType);
      CustLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Customer No.", BilltoCustomerNo);
      CustLedgerEntry.SETRANGE("Document No.", DocumentNo);
      IF CustLedgerEntry.FINDFIRST THEN
        EXIT(CustLedgerEntry."Entry No.");
    END;

    PROCEDURE GetPlantLocationInvoiceCopies@1100485000() : Integer;
    VAR
      PlantSetup@1100485000 : Record 11012550;
      PlantLocation@1100485001 : Record 11012554;
      SalesInvoiceLine@1100485002 : Record 113;
      Customer@1100485003 : Record 18;
      FPSLicenseManagement@1100527400 : Codeunit 11229289;
    BEGIN
      IF (NOT "Sales Invoice Header"."Plant Invoice") THEN
        EXIT(0);

      IF (NOT FPSLicenseManagement.LicenseAndReadPermissionForTable(PlantSetup)) OR
         (NOT FPSLicenseManagement.LicenseAndReadPermissionForTable(PlantLocation))
      THEN
        EXIT(0);

      IF (NOT PlantSetup.GET) THEN
        EXIT(0);

      IF PlantSetup."Level One Loc. per Invoice" = PlantSetup."Level One Loc. per Invoice"::Setup THEN BEGIN
        IF (NOT PlantSetup."One Location per Invoice") THEN
          EXIT(0);
      END ELSE BEGIN
        IF NOT Customer.GET("Sales Invoice Header"."Bill-to Customer No.") THEN
          EXIT(0);
        IF (NOT Customer."One Location per Plant Invoice") THEN
          EXIT(0);
      END;

      SalesInvoiceLine.SETRANGE("Document No.", "Sales Invoice Header"."No.");
      SalesInvoiceLine.SETFILTER(Type, '<>%1', SalesInvoiceLine.Type::" ");
      SalesInvoiceLine.SETFILTER("Plant Location", '<>%1', '');
      IF SalesInvoiceLine.FINDFIRST THEN BEGIN
        IF PlantLocation.GET(SalesInvoiceLine."Plant Location") THEN BEGIN
          SalesInvoiceLine.FILTERGROUP(6);
          SalesInvoiceLine.SETFILTER("Plant Location", '<>%1', SalesInvoiceLine."Plant Location");
          IF NOT SalesInvoiceLine.FINDFIRST THEN
            EXIT(PlantLocation."Invoice Copies");
        END;
      END;

      EXIT(0);
    END;

    BEGIN
    END.
  }

  <Code>Public Function BlankZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    If Value = 0 Then
        Return ""
    End If
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    If Value &gt; 0 Then
        Return ""
    End If
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankZeroAndPos(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    If Value &gt;= 0 Then
        Return ""
    End If
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNeg(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    If Value &lt; 0 Then
        Return ""
    End If
    Return Value
End Function

Public Function BlankNegAndZero(ByVal Value As Decimal)
    If Value &lt;= 0 Then
        Return ""
    End If
    Return Value
End Function

Shared offset As Integer
Shared newgroup As Object
Shared currentgroup1 As Object
Shared currentgroup2 As Object

Public Function GetGroupPageNumber(newgroup2 As Boolean, pagenumber As Integer) As Object
    If newgroup2
        offset = pagenumber - 1
    End If
    Return pagenumber - offset
End Function

Public Function InNewGroup(group1 As Object, group2 As Object) As Boolean
    newgroup = False
    If Not (group1 = currentgroup1)
        newgroup = True
        currentgroup2 = group2
        currentgroup1 = group1
    Else
        If Not (group2 = currentgroup2)
            newgroup = True
            currentgroup2 = group2
        End If
    End If
    Return newgroup
End Function

Shared Data1 As Object

Public Function GetData(Num As Integer) As Object
    Return Cstr(Choose(Num, Split(Cstr(Data1), Chr(177))))
End Function

Public Function SetData(NewData As Object)
    If NewData &lt;&gt; "" Then
        Data1 = NewData
    End If
End Function


Shared Data2 As Decimal

Public Function GetData2() As Decimal
    Return Data2
End Function

Public Function SetData2(Reset As Boolean, NewData As Decimal) As Boolean
    If (NewData &lt;&gt; 0) Or Reset Then
        Data2 = NewData
    End If
    Return True
End Function


Shared LinesPrinted As Boolean

Public Function SetLinesPrinted(NewData As Boolean) As Boolean
    LinesPrinted = NewData
    Return True
End Function

Public Function GetLinesPrinted() As Boolean
    Return LinesPrinted
End Function

</Code>
  <Language>=User!Language</Language>
  <ConsumeContainerWhitespace>true</ConsumeContainerWhitespace>
  <rd:ReportUnitType>Cm</rd:ReportUnitType>
</Report>
    END_OF_RDLDATA
